
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 For producing the improvement of the microorganism nitrilase of the fixation of glycolic 
 
 Technical field 
 The present invention relates to the synthesis of organic acid and microbiological arts.More specifically, providing a method to improve the specific activity that glycollic nitrile is hydrolyzed to glycolic by the dehydration enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity after aquation again.Particularly, it provides a method, before being dehydrated: there is the enzyme catalyst of nitrilase activity with glutaraldehyde pretreatment, the pretreated cell of glutaraldehyde is fixed and is chemically crosslinked fixed cell.After aquation again, for the enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity that those pass through dehydration and again aquation but do not carry out the process, enzyme catalyst of the invention shows improved nitrilase specific activity.  
 
 
 Background technique 
 Glycolic (HOCH 2 COOH；CAS Registry Number is 79-14-1) be carboxylic acid 'alpha '-hydroxy acids family simplest member.The property of glycolic makes it have the consumption and industrial application of ideal wide scope, including being used for well recovery, leather industry, oil and gas industry, laundry and textile industry, preparing polyglycolic acid (PGA), and the ingredient as personal care product as monomer.Glycolic or a variety of industrial detergent (dairy produce and food processing equipment detergents, household and mechanism detergent, industrial cleaners [be used for transporting equipment, stone skill, printed circuit board, stainless steel boiler and processing equipment, cooling tower/heat exchanger] and intermetallic composite coating [being polished for pickling of metal, the polishing of copper, etching, plating, electrolysis method]) main component.Also it is reported that glycolic can be used as gas barrier material (showing the oxygen barrier characteristic of height) for sheathing foodstuff and soda (2005/106005 A1 of WO).But the traditional chemical of glycolic is synthetically produced a large amount of impurity, must be driven off these impurity before use.Industry is there is an urgent need to commercially produce the new technology of glycolic, especially with the new technology of low cost production high purity ethanol acid.  
 It is corresponding carboxylic acid (such as glycolic) that micro bioenzyme catalysis agent, which is able to use nitrilase (EC 3.5.5.7) for nitrile (such as glycollic nitrile) direct hydrolysis, wherein not generating corresponding amide intermediate (reaction equation 1)；Or nitrile (such as glycollic nitrile) can be hydrolyzed to corresponding carboxylic acid (such as glycolic) with the combination of amidase (EC 3.5.1.4) by nitrile hydratase (EC 4.2.1.84), wherein nitrile hydratase (NHase) converts amide for nitrile first, and then amide is converted to corresponding carboxylic acid (reaction equation 2) by amidase: 
 
 
 
 The enzymatic hydrolysis of nitrile to glycolic for commercial object needs to generate the enzyme catalyst of high volume by fermentation.Most water contents in fermentation liquid in these volumes.Due to the reason of the high volume fermentation liquid, thus include the fermentation liquid of enzyme catalyst storage and (in many cases) transport cause logistics and economically the problem of.The principle for providing the simplicity in the storage and transport of enzyme catalyst is to separate enzyme from fermentation liquid, enzyme catalyst is fixed (for example, retaining by carrageenan gel), and fixed enzyme catalyst is dehydrated.For can be by fixed enzyme catalyst again aquation before producing glycolic.But dehydration and again aquation often cause the loss of serious enzymatic activity.  
 It is described previously the dehydration or drying of fixed cell catalyst.US 5,998,180 describe the method for generating the microorganism nitrilase of dry fixation, wherein prunosus red coccus (Rhodococcus rhodochrous) NCIMB 40757 or 408333 cell of NCIMB containing the nitrilase remain its at least 80% initial activity after the polyacrylamide pearl for being fixed on crosslinking；After the dry humidity to 12% of 60 DEG C of polyacrylamide pearls by crosslinking, the Cell Nitrilase of generated fixation remains its at least 90% initial fixed activity.B.DeGiulio et al. (World J.Microbiol.Biotechnol.21:739-746, (2005)) fixation of the lactic acid bacteria in calcium alginate is described, then the cell catalyst of the fixation of generation is lyophilized, wherein at least 72% cell remains metabolic activity after freeze drying.US 5,846,762 describes the dehydration of the gelatin pearl containing covalently fixed cellobiase, and record in the 6th column 9-11 row: once after dehydration, calcium alginate and kappa carrageenan pearl generally cannot be by aquations again.  
 Then what is be described immediately above is dehydrated or is lyophilized the improvement of no one of method of aquation report enzymatic activity that aquation recycles later again again by fixed enzyme catalyst, or when the enzyme catalyst of generated aquation again is applied to convert a substrate into the reaction of product, the improvement of the stability of enzymatic activity (compared with not being the enzyme catalyst by the fixation of the comparable aquation again of the pretreated cell preparation of glutaraldehyde).  
 The enzymatic hydrolysis of glycollic nitrile to glycolic usually requires the glycollic nitrile of substantially pure form other than (such as in the case where dehydration/aquation again) lead to enzyme catalyst loss of activity due to enzyme catalyst processing.Method (the US 2,175,805 of the reaction the synthesis of glycolonitrile by the aqueous solution of formaldehyde and hydrogen cyanide was once reported in the past；US 2,890,238；With US 5,187,301；Reaction equation 3).  
 
 
 
 But, these methods generally produce aqueous glycollic nitrile reaction product, it needs to carry out depth purifying (such as distillation purifying), because many impurity and/or the by-product (including extra reactant formaldehyde) of reaction may interfere with the enzymatic conversion method of glycollic nitrile to glycolic, including inhibit catalyst activity (i.e. reduction specific activity).Particularly, it is known that formaldehyde can generate undesired modification (Metz et al. and reacting with the amino group of the side chain from -terminal amino acid residue and arginine, cysteine, histidine and lysine residue in albumen, J.Biol.Chem., 279 (8): 6235-6243 (2004)).The inhibition of catalyst activity reduces the overall productivity (i.e. the total grams for the glycolic that every gram of catalyst is formed) of catalyst, and this dramatically increases the costs of overall process, so that Production by Enzymes may be economically impractical compared with chemical synthesis.Therefore, it is necessary to such reaction conditions: its can defence enzyme activity with resist those reduce catalyst activities undesired impurity.  
 It has been reported that by the way that formaldehyde is carried out heat treatment to generate method (US 11/3143865 and the US 11/314905 of high purity ethanol nitrile before glycollic nitrile synthetic reaction；Reaction equation 3).But glycollic nitrile can be reversibly broken down into formaldehyde and hydrogen cyanide.Therefore, there is still a need for protection nitrilase activity is to resist the ill effect for decomposing the formaldehyde and hydrogen cyanide that generate by glycollic nitrile.  
 US 5,508,181 also describes relevant to the rapid inactivation of enzyme catalyst similar difficult when converting 'alpha '-hydroxy acids for nitrile compound.Specifically, 5 US, 508,181 record: according to dissociation, alpha-hydroxy nitrile compound decomposed is corresponding aldehyde.It is reported that these aldehyde and with protein binding in a short time by enzyme-deactivating, therefore, it is difficult to obtain the 'alpha '-hydroxy acids or Alpha-hydroxy amide (the 2nd column, 16-29 row) of high concentration with high productivity from alpha-hydroxy nitrile.Make the means of enzyme-deactivating as the accumulation due to aldehyde is prevented, phosphate or hypophosphites ion are added into reaction mixture.Similarly, US 5,326,702 is described using sulphite, dithionite or dithionite ion trap aldehyde and is prevented enzyme-deactivating, but it concludes that and is also insufficient for most commercial objects even if the concentration using such additive, produced and accumulation 'alpha '-hydroxy acids.  
 In addition, U.S.6,037,155 introduction: the low accumulation of 'alpha '-hydroxy acids product is related with the enzyme-deactivating in the short time caused by the accumulation of the aldehyde of decomposition.In hydrogen cyanide, (alpha-hydroxy nitrile decomposed generates hydrogen cyanide (Mowry in water and corresponding aldehydes or ketones for these inventors prompt, David T., Chemical Reviews, Vol.42,189-283 pages (1948))) in the presence of enzymatic activity be suppressed (Asano et al., AgriculturalBiological Chemistry, Vol.46,1165-1174 pages (1982)).Inventor solves the problems, such as the enzyme-deactivating of aldehyde induction by using microorganism (its enzymatic activity can be modified and cyanogen substance is added into reaction mixture).The addition of cyanogen substance limits decomposition of the alpha-hydroxy nitrile to aldehyde and hydrogen cyanide.Although this strategy provides benefit to system, but it addresses only the relevant one aspect of the enzyme-deactivating being converted into glycolic to glycollic nitrile, that is, as described above, known glycollic nitrile is reversibly decomposed into hydrogen cyanide and formaldehyde, and the two is known to have negative effects to enzyme catalyst activity.  
 Protection has the specific activity of the enzyme catalyst of nitrilase activity (referring to the U.S. Patent application XX/XXXXXX (CL3584) of same applicant when having developed a kind of individual method to convert glycolic for glycollic nitrile there are formaldehyde; it is incorporated herein by reference); wherein by the way that amine protective agent is added into reaction mixture or by the way that nitrilase catalyst to be fixed in matrix (containing amine protective agent, such as PEI, polyallylamine, PVOH/ polyvinylamine etc.) to or obtained in matrix significantly improving for catalyst activity and stability.Within the system, the specific activity of the catalyst in the presence of formaldehyde is improved.  
 Although method described above much all improves nitrilase catalyst for the productivity of glycolic, but when the catalyst is used for the hydrolysis of Hydrolysis alcohol nitrile (such as, the initial stage of slot type reaction (CSTR) or fixed bed column reactor is continuously stirred in the continuous batch reaction with catalyst circulation, or in starting) usually still observe that the initial enzyme activity of fixed microorganism nitrilase is remarkably decreased.Solve the problems, such as that nitrilase activity initial in glycollic nitrile hydrolytic process is remarkably decreased (as described in the U.S. Patent application XX/XXXXXX (CL3888) of same applicant by pre-processing microbial catalyst part before being fixed on carrageenan with glutaraldehyde, it is incorporated herein by reference), wherein remaining the initially fixed microorganism nitrilase specific activity (μm ole number for the glycollic nitrile that every gram of catalyst hydrolyzes per minute) of significantly higher percentage during glycollic nitrile is hydrolyzed to glycolic (as ammonium salt).  
 U.S.4,288,552 record (the 1st column, 46-49 row and the 2nd column, 50-55 row): glutaraldehyde sensibility enzyme (such as sulfydryl enzyme (such as nitrilase) and other enzymes in the active site of enzyme molecule or the place of very close active site with SH group) is inactivated by sulfydryl reactive reagent such as glutaraldehyde.Therefore, the not only unpredictable significant decrease that will not cause microorganism nitrilase activity with the enzyme catalyst of nitrilase activity with glutaraldehyde pretreatment before fixing, it is surprised to find that it is beneficial for being pre-processed with glutaraldehyde for enzyme catalyst activity instead, before glycollic nitrile is hydrolyzed to glycolic, when fixed enzyme catalyst is dehydrated aquation again then.Method of the invention prevents the significant loss of activity in hydration step of dehydration/again, and the enzyme catalyst of the fixation of aquation again is generated, which has initial activity and the active subsequent stability of enzyme catalyst when the enzymatic activity of the subsequent fixation by aquation again is used to convert glycolic for glycollic nitrile.The method that this benefit is incorporated herein description --- which solve the needs of business process, including dehydration, for generating the enzyme catalyst with improved specific activity (for producing glycolic after aquation again).  
 Therefore, problem to be solved is: needing a kind of viable commercial method with for generating the enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity, for glycollic nitrile to be hydrolyzed to glycolic with improved specific activity.More specifically, a kind of commercially acceptable method is needed to use the enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity that glycollic nitrile is hydrolyzed to glycolic, makes due to the dehydration before using and aquation and decompositions due to impurity or reactant cause the minimization of loss of enzymatic activity caused by inactivating again.  
 
 
 Summary of the invention 
 Current problem is by providing the fixation enzyme catalyst for generating the dehydration after aquation again with improved specific activity and the method that the enzyme catalyst is used to convert glycollic nitrile to glycolic achieving a solution, which comprises 
 (a) enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity is generated by fermentation；  
 (b) enzyme catalyst is pre-processed with glutaraldehyde；  
 (c) optionally unreacted glutaraldehyde is inactivated with bisulfites after glutaraldehyde pretreatment；  
 (d) enzyme catalyst is recycled from (b) or (c) and the enzyme catalyst is fixed in carrageenan；  
 (e) carrageenan-fixation enzyme catalyst generated in (d) is crosslinked with glutaraldehyde and polyethyleneimine；With 
 (f) enzyme catalyst by the fixation of the crosslinking generated in step (e) is dehydrated.  
 Another aspect of the present invention is in aqueous solution by the catalyst of the fixation of the dehydration of above step (f) again aquation.In addition, the enzyme catalyst of the aquation again is contacted with glycollic nitrile in aqueous solution, to generate glycolic.On the other hand, glycolic is recycled from the aqueous solution.  
 When for when converting glycolic (as ammonium salt) for glycollic nitrile, in fixation, crosslinking, dehydration and enzyme catalyst is not pre-processed using glutaraldehyde before aquation again for the enzyme catalyst of fixation for preparing relative to those, its initial specific activity (μm ole number for the glycollic nitrile that every gram of catalyst hydrolyzes per minute) of significantly higher percentage is remained by the enzyme catalyst of above step a) to the method f) fixation generated.  
 Another aspect of the present invention is the enzyme catalyst being dehydrated as the improved enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity.The enzyme catalyst of the dehydration retains at least about 70%, at least about 75%, at least about 80%, at least about 85% or at least about the 90% of its specific activity after aquation again.

 Detailed description of the invention 
 Provide the method for the specific activity of a kind of fixation of dehydration for improving and there is nitrilase activity and crosslinking the enzyme catalyst for glycollic nitrile to be hydrolyzed to glycolic after aquation again.Particularly, provide a method that there is the enzyme catalyst of nitrilase activity with glutaraldehyde pretreatment, the pretreated cell of glutaraldehyde is fixed and is chemically crosslinked fixed cell, be then dehydrated.After aquation again, the pretreated fixation of glutaraldehyde and crosslinking enzyme catalyst relative to those by dehydration and again aquation but the fixation with nitrilase activity for not carrying out the process and crosslinking enzyme catalyst for, show improved nitrilase specific activity.

 Some terms and abbreviation have been used in the disclosure.Following definitions apply unless specifically stated otherwise.

 The term " about " of the quantity of ingredient used in the modification present invention used herein or reaction reagent refers to that the difference of numerical quantities, the difference may come from, for example, compound concentration or typical measurement and liquid operation sequence when using solution in objective world；Casual mistake in these programs；Prepare manufacturer, source or the purity of ingredient used when composition or implementation method；Etc..Term " about " further includes the quantitative difference as caused by the different equilibrium conditions of the composition from specific original mixture.Whether it is modified with term " about ", claim includes the equivalent of quantity.In one embodiment, term " about " is meant within the 10% of the numerical value of report, the preferably within the 5% of the numerical value of report 
 The term as used herein " glycollic nitrile " is abbreviated as " GLN ", and all other synonymous object with hydroxyacetonitrile, 2- hydroxyacetonitrile, methylol nitrile and CAS Registry Number 107-16-4 is synonymous.  
 The term as used herein " glycolic " is abbreviated as " GLA ", and all other synonymous object with hydroxyacetic acid (hydroxyaceticacid), hydroxyacetic acid (hydroxyethanoic acid) and CAS Registry Number 79-14-1 is synonymous.The glycolic generated according to the method for the present invention can be the form of protonated carboxylic acid and/or corresponding ammonium salt.  
 The term as used herein " alcohol acid phosphate " is abbreviated as " NH 4 GLA”。  
 The term as used herein " hydroxyl acetamide " is that ammonia reacts the amide generated with glycolic, refers to all other synonymous object of the compound with CAS Registry Number 598-42-5.  
 The term as used herein " glycolide " refers to the compound of CAS Registry Number 502-97-6.  
 The term as used herein " formaldehyde " is abbreviated as " FA ", and all other synonymous object with formaldehyde, methyl aldehyde, oxygen methane and CAS Registry Number 50-00-0 is synonymous.Formaldehyde commercially generally comprises oligomer (the typically about 1wt% to about 15wt%) of monomer formaldehyde (" free formaldehyde ") and various formaldehyde and some methanol.  
 All other synonymous object of the term as used herein " hydrogen cyanide " and cyanic acid, hydrogen cyanide and CAS Registry Number 200-821-6 is synonymous.  
 The term as used herein " glutaraldehyde " is abbreviated as " GA ", itself and glutaraldehyde (pentanedial), 1,5- glutaraldehyde (1,5-pentanedial), 1,5- pentanedione (1,5-pentanedione), glutaraldehyde (diglutaric aldehyde), glutaraldehyde (glutaral), glutaraldehyde (glutardialdehyde), glutaric acid dialdehyde (glutaric acid dialdehyde), glutaraldehyde (glutaric dialdehyde) and CAS Registry Number 111-30-8 all other synonymous object be synonymous.  
 The term as used herein " bisulfites " or " sodium hydrogensulfite " and sodium sulfite salt, sulfurous acid mono-sodium salt, sodium hydrogensulfite (hydrogen sodium sulfite), sodium hydrogensulfite (hydrogensulfite sodium), sulfurous acid list sodium, sodium acid sulfite, sodium hydrogensulfite (sodium bisulfite), sodium bisulfate (sodium bisulphate), sodium hydrogensulfite (sodium hydrogen sulfite), all other synonymous object of sodium sulfite (sodium sulfite) (NaHSO3) and CAS Registry Number 7631-90-5 are synonymous.  
 The term as used herein " recycling " means separation, purifies or be displaced through the product that method of the invention is formed.The method of separation and purified product is well-known in the art from reaction mixture, including but not limited to selective precipitation, crystallization, filtering, reactive solvents extraction, ion exchange, electrodialysis, polymerization, distillation, thermal decomposition, alcoholysis, column chromatography and combinations thereof.In one embodiment, term " recycling " can also include that product mixtures (usually after filtering out enzyme catalyst) are transferred to another reaction to generate one or more other products.In a preferred embodiment, glycolic is recycled using ion exchange.  
 The term as used herein " enzyme catalyst ", " nitrilase catalyst " or " microbial cell catalyst " refers to such catalyst, it is characterised in that with the nitrilase activity for converting glycollic nitrile to glycolic and ammonia (i.e. comprising at least one polypeptide with nitrilase activity).Nitrile (preferably aliphatic nitrile) is converted into corresponding carboxylic acid by nitrilase, does not form the corresponding amide as intermediate (see reaction equation 1).Nitrilase has several conservative sign structure known in the art domains jointly, is included herein the sign structure domain of referred to as " catalysis flag sequence " or " flag sequence ".The region includes required cysteine residues (such as the Cys of SEQ ID NO:4 164 ).It therefore, can be by whether identifying the polypeptide with nitrilase activity there are catalyst structure domain flag sequence (SEQ ID NO:1).In a preferred embodiment, flag sequence is SEQ ID NO:2.Enzyme catalyst can be the form of (permeabilized) microbial cell of entire microbial cell or permeabilization." enzyme catalyst of recycling " used herein refers to the enzyme catalyst reused in batch or successive reaction as enzyme catalyst.The step of depending on generation described herein or using the method for enzyme catalyst, enzyme catalyst can be the crosslinking of the pretreated fixation of glutaraldehyde and dehydration or again aquation.

 " promoter " is the DNA sequence dna for referring to the expression of control coded sequence or functional r NA.Generally, coded sequence is located at 3 ' ends of promoter sequence.Promoter can derive from ortho states gene with complete form, or the different elements by being originated from the different promoters naturally found form, it might even be possible to the DNA fragmentation comprising synthesis.The promoter of gene expression is caused to be commonly known as " constitutive promoter " in most cases or under most environmental conditions in most cell types.The promoter of gene expression is only caused to be commonly known as " inducible promoters " in the presence of specific compound or environmental condition.Since the exact boundary of regulating and controlling sequence in most cases has been fully defined, so the DNA fragmentation of different length can have identical promoter activity.  
 The term as used herein " being operably connected " refer to the nucleic acid sequence on single nucleic acid molecules by the function of a sequence by another influenced in the way of connect.For example, promoter is to be operably connected with coded sequence when promoter can influence the expression of coded sequence (i.e. coded sequence is under the transcription control of promoter).Coded sequence can be operably connected according to sense or antisense with regulating and controlling sequence.

 Enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity 
 
 All nitrilases (EC 3.5.5.7) all have conservative catalytic triads (Glu, Lys and Cys) (Chauhan et al., Appl.Microbiol.Biotechnol.61:118-122 (2003)；2 (1) Pace, H.andBrenner, C., Genome Biol. [online computer file]: reviews0001.1-0001.9 (2001)).All known nitrilases have cysteine (Cowan et al., Extremophiles, the 2:207-216 (1998) of nucleophilic in enzyme active sites；Pace, H.and Brenner, C., see on；With Chauhan et al., see on) and it is all sensitive to the inactivation of sulfydryl reactant (copper chloride, silver nitrate, mercuric acetate or the iron chloride of 1.0mM concentration each cause declining to a great extent for Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase enzymatic activity).Cysteine residues can also be irreversibly oxidized to sulfinic acid, lead to the loss of enzymatic activity.Although nitrilase has sensibility to various Inactivations, fixed Acidovorax facilis 72W cell is strong (robust), its most of nitrilase activity (US 6,870,038 can be retained after multiple circular responses；U.S.7,148,051；U.S.7,198,927；With Chauhan et al., see on).Also have shown that the conversion of nitrilase catalyst catalysis alpha-hydroxy nitrile (i.e. glycollic nitrile) from Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase to alpha-hydroxy carboxylic acid compounds (i.e. glycolic) (referring to US 6,383,786；US6,416,980；And U.S.7,198,927).  
 It has been reported that Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase (US 6,870,038 compared with the sequence of other bacterial enzyme nitriles；Chauhan et al., see on).72W nitrilase has several conservative sign structures domain, the catalysis region (the amino acid residue 160-171 of SEQ IDNO:4) in the region (the amino acid residue 40-55 of SEQ ID NO:4) including 16 amino acid at amino terminal and 12 amino acid containing required cysteine residues.This required cysteine residues (Cys of SEQ ID NO:4 164 ) and conservative the glutamic acid (Glu of SEQ ID NO:4 48 ) and the lysine residue (Lys of SEQID NO:4 130 ) it is formed in the catalytic triads motif (Pace, H., and Brenner, C., see on) found in all nitrilases.  
 Region around each catalytic triads residue is highly conserved, especially around catalytic cysteine residues region.Required catalytic cysteine residues, which are located at, to be referred to as in " catalysis mark motif " or the well-conserved region of " mark motif ".Therefore; it includes that (runic represents strict conservation acidic amino acid residue to formula 1 that this method, which can be used for protecting; Italicized residues are the residues little change of less amino acid residue [i.e. 3 or] for showing minimum changeability, are lined out below catalytic cysteine residues) enzymatic activity of any nitrilase of catalysis mark motif that defines: 
 Formula 1 (SEQ ID NO:1) 
 Gly-Xaa 1 -Xaa 2 -Xaa 3 - Cys -Trp-Glu-Xaa 4 -Xaa 5 -Xaa 6 -Xaa 7 -Xaa 8   
 Wherein 
 Xaa1=Ala or Gly；  
 Xaa2=Leu, Val or Ala；  
 Xaa3=Ala, Asn, Ile, Cys, Val or Gln；  
 Xaa4=His or Asn；  
 Xaa5=Leu, Tyr, Phe, Ala, Met, Lys, Val, Thr or Arg；  
 Xaa6=Asn, Gln, Met, Leu or Ser；  
 Xaa7=Pro or Thr；With 
 Xaa8=Leu or Val.  
 In a preferred embodiment, the nitrilase mark motif of formula 1 is Xaa 1 =Ala or Gly；Xaa 2 =Leu；Xaa 3 =Ala, Asn, Ile, Cys, Val or Gln；Xaa 4 =His；Xaa 5 =Leu, Tyr, Phe, Ala, Met, Lys, Val, Thr or Arg；Xaa 6 =Ser, Gln, Asn or Met；Xaa 7 =Pro；And Xaa 8 =Leu；To generate catalysis mark motif represented by the formula: 
 Gly-Xaa 1 -Leu-Xaa 3 -Cys-Trp-Glu-His-Xaa 5 -Xaa 6 - Pro-Leu (SEQ ID NO:2).  
 The example of nitrilase is provided in table 1, sequence and position including being catalyzed mark motif sequence accordingly.

 Acidovorax facilis 72W (ATCC 55746) nitrilase 
 
 Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase (EC 3.5.5.1) is the strong catalyst (WO 01/75077 that carboxylic acid is generated from aliphatic or aromatic nitrile；US 6,870,038；With Chauhan et al., see on).It has also shown it and is catalyzed the conversion of alpha-hydroxy nitrile (i.e. glycollic nitrile) to alpha-hydroxy carboxylic acid compounds (i.e. glycolic) (referring to US 6,383,786；With US 6,416,980).But the nitrilase catalyst when glycollic nitrile is converted to glycolic with improved nitrilase activity and/or stability (relative to Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase) will reduce the cost of production glycolic.Therefore, it can be used for reducing the cost of production glycolic using the method for improved nitrilase catalyst production glycolic.But Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase is the improved nitrilase of the enzyme catalyst for this method purpose and above-detailed.  
 
 The industrial production of microbial catalyst 
 
 When needing to carry out the commodity production of enzyme catalyst described herein, a variety of cultural methods can be used.Method well known in the art can be used, fermentation operation (Thomas D.Brock in is carried out with batch, fedbatch or continuous mode Biotechnology:A Textbook of IndustrialMicrobiology , Second Edition (1989) Sinauer Associates, Inc., Sunderland, MA, (1989)；Deshpande, Mukund V., Appl.Biochem.Biotechnol.36 (3): 227-234 (1992)).  
 Classical batch experiments method is closed system, wherein the ingredient of culture medium is set when cultivating and starting, during the cultivation process without manual change.Therefore, when incubation starts by the bacterization of needs to culture medium and allow its grow or generate metabolic activity (any substance is not added into system).But generally, " batch " culture is batch added in carbon source meaning, it is often necessary to attempt to control some factor such as pH and oxygen concentration.In batch system, the metabolin and components of biomass of system persistently change, until culture terminates.In batch experiments, cell slowly reaches high-speed rapid growth logarithmic phase from the static delay phase, eventually arrives at stationary phase, reduces or stops in stationary phase growth rate.If not handling, the cell in stationary phase finally will be dead.In some systems, the cell in logarithmic phase is generally responsible for mass production final product or intermediate.It can be produced after stationary phase or exponential phase in other systems.  
 Fedbatch system is the variant of standard batch system.Fed-batch process is also suitable for the present invention, and it includes typical batch systems, only with the investment for gradually increase substrate of incubation.When catabolite repression tends to inhibit the metabolism of cell and needs to limit the quantity of substrate in culture medium, fedbatch system is useful.Practical concentration of substrate in fedbatch system is difficult to measure, therefore based on can survey factor (such as pH, dissolved oxygen and exhaust gas (such as CO 2 ) partial pressure) and variation assess.Batch and fed-batch method be it is common be also well known in the art, example can be found in Brock (see on) and Deshpande (see on).  
 The commodity production of the enzyme catalyst of the invention with nitrilase can also be realized by continuously cultivating.Continuous culture is open system, wherein being continuously added to determining culture medium, while into bioreactor in order to handle the conditioned culture media for removing equivalent.Cell is usually maintained at constant high density of liquid phase by continuous culture, and wherein cell is mostly in logarithmic growth phase.Alternatively, can continuously be cultivated with fixed cell, wherein being continuously added to carbon and nutrients and continuously removing useful product, by-product or waste products from cellular material.The fixation that many kinds of solids support (being made of natural and/or synthetic material) carries out cell can be used.  
 Continuously or semi-continuously culture allows to adjust the factor or any number of factor for influencing cell growth or final cell concentration.For example, limiting nutrient object (such as carbon source or nitrogen level) is maintained at fixed rate and all other parameter is allowed to slow down by a kind of method.In other systems, it can continue to change some factors for influencing growth but keep cell concentration (according to culture solution turbidimetry) constant.Continuous system makes great efforts to keep stable state growth conditions, thus must keep excluding as culture solution in culture and caused by balance between loss cell and cell growth rate.Adjust the nutrients of culture of continuous cultivation and the method for growth factor and make the maximized technology of the generating rate of cell in industrial microorganism field be it is well known, a variety of such methods are described in detail in Brock (see on).  
 Fermentation medium of the invention must contain suitable carbon substrate.Suitable substrate can include but is not limited to: monosaccharide such as glucose and fructose, disaccharides such as lactose or sucrose, polysaccharide such as or mixtures thereof starch or cellulose, and come from the unpurified mixture of renewable raw materials (such as cheese whey penetrant, corn steep liquor, beet molasses and barley malt).Accordingly, it is considered to may include a variety of containing carbon substrate to carbon source used in the present invention, this will only be limited by the selection of organism.  
 
 Enzyme catalyst is pre-processed with glutaraldehyde before fixing 
 
 With glutaraldehyde processing enzyme catalyst fermentation culture medium be kill culture in microorganism to avoid pollution and to living body recombination culture it is relevant operation, storage and transport aspect safety problem short-cut method.It has now been discovered that being pre-processed with glutaraldehyde or being able to maintain the nitrilase activity in suspension and the cell of fixed form after pre-processing with glutaraldehyde with bisulf iotate-treated.  
 Keep nitrilase activity by time, the influence of temperature, glutaraldehyde concentration, pH and inhibition product (such as the other amine (such as amino acid and peptide) to interact in ammonia and culture solution with glutaraldehyde) concentration and pre-processing enzyme catalyst with glutaraldehyde.Preferred glutaraldehyde preprocess method handles the cell (100-150OD from high density fermentation with the glutaraldehyde of the 5-10wt% in water 550 ), glutaraldehyde in the water is preferably in the case where being sufficiently mixed with 50mg to 500mg glutaraldehyde/L-min conveying, with 50mg to 200mg glutaraldehyde/L-min conveying more preferably in the case where being sufficiently mixed, with 50mg to 100mg glutaraldehyde/L-min conveying most preferably in the case where being sufficiently mixed, to generate about 3g to about 5g glutaraldehyde/L final concentration (about 0.025g to about 0.042g glutaraldehyde/OD 550 ), more preferably from about 3.6g to about 5g glutaraldehyde/L final concentration (about 0.030g to about 0.042g glutaraldehyde/OD 550 ).The pretreated culture of glutaraldehyde can be held in fermentor about 1 to 5 hour.Then the aqueous solution of sodium bisulfite of 10wt% is optionally added so that remaining glutaraldehyde inactivation with 1g/L.  
 The pretreated preferred pH of the glutaraldehyde of enzyme catalyst is pH5.0 to 9.0, more preferably pH5.0 to 8.0 in fermentation liquid or cell suspending liquid, and still more preferably from pH5.0 to 7.0, still more preferably from pH5.0 to 6.0, most candidate is pH5.0 to 5.5.The pretreated remaining glutaraldehyde concentration of glutaraldehyde is usually lower, within the scope of 10-200ppm, can as described above be inactivated remaining glutaraldehyde by the way that the final concentration of bisulfites to about 1g/L is added.It was found that glutaraldehyde and bisulfites pretreatment do not have conspicuousness ill-effect for nitrilase activity.Optionally, glutaraldehyde or the pretreated cell suspending liquid of glutaraldehyde/bisulfites are cooled to 5-10 DEG C, optionally with water or suitable store buffer liquid washing (carrying out by being concentrated with diluting cells suspension again or fermentation liquid) to remove remaining bisulfites and unreacted glutaraldehyde.  
 
 The fixation and chemical crosslinking of the pretreated enzyme catalyst of glutaraldehyde 
 
 The method for largely having reported fixed enzyme catalyst, these methods to it is known to those skilled in the art (Methods in Biotechnology, Vol.1: Immobilization of Enzymes and Cells ；Gordon F.Bickerstaff, Editor；Humana Press, Totowa, NJ, USA；1997).In the past it has also been reported that the fixation (US 6,870,038) of Acidovorax facilis 72W nitrilase catalyst.  
 Furthermore, there are also fixed then in glutaraldehyde/polyethyleneimine crosslinking fixed enzyme catalyst method (such as in  US  6 in carrageenan, 870, it is disclosed in 038 and in  US  6, it as being described in detail in 551,804B, is incorporated herein by reference), but it will be appreciated by those of ordinary skill in the art that change can be applicable in easily simultaneously to complete fixed and be crosslinked.It is described to change the range for considering within this paper and falling into this method.In addition, the quantity or concentration for fixed and chemical crosslinking ingredient will be according to the quantity and type change of enzyme catalyst and the tunning of enzyme catalyst.It will be appreciated by those of ordinary skill in the art that these factors and correspondingly adjustment are fixed and are chemically crosslinked program.It is chemically crosslinked about with glutaraldehyde and polyethyleneimine, US 6,551,804 describes the methods and procedures of the fixed cell of chemical crosslinking alginates (see on).It is described to describe to be also applied for the cell that the carrageenan of this paper is fixed.  
 
 The aquation of the dehydration of the fixed micro bioenzyme catalysis agent of the carrageenan of glutaraldehyde/polyethyleneimine crosslinking/again 
 
 As described above, the application one relevant to microorganism nitrilase catalyst is used special problem to be solved is the storage and transport of enzyme catalyst.The aspect to be considered includes related to the volume of material in the storage and transport of enzyme catalyst with nitrilase activity and the enzymatic activity with material inactivates relevant difficulty at any time.When being fixed on carrageenan and then when being crosslinked with glutaraldehyde and polyethyleneimine, the microorganism nitrilase catalyst of generated fixation contains the water of about 90% weight, catalyst be normally stored in 5 DEG C etc. in the aqueous buffer solution of weight.The reduction of water present in fixed microorganism nitrilase catalyst and the reduction of the aqueous buffer solution for storing catalyst will reduce the volume of the catalyst and relevant buffers that need to transport and store before use, further significantly improve the economic factor of glycolic production.  
 The dehydration of the enzyme catalyst of glutaraldehyde/polyethyleneimine crosslinking fixation can be realized by any method known to those skilled in the art, these methods include but is not limited to, it is dehydrated, is dehydrated in inert gas flow, is dehydrated in the vacuum tank purged with or without inert gas (such as nitrogen or argon gas) in air, or freeze-drying (freeze-dried).Preferably about 5 DEG C to about 60 DEG C of the temperature of dehydration, more preferably about 15 DEG C to about 50 DEG C, most preferably about 20 DEG C to about 40 DEG C.The pearl weight of generated dehydration can reduce by about 91% (cell containing microorganism nitrilase that pearl when beginning contains about 5% stem cell weight) than its initial weight in wet base.The cell catalyst of the fixation of dehydration can be stored in air or inert gas, and storage temperature is preferably -25 DEG C to 35 DEG C, preferably 5 DEG C to 25 DEG C.Can by by the pearl of dehydration be placed in water or suitable aqueous buffer solution (such as pH be 7.3 0.10M alcohol acid phosphate solution) in by the cell catalyst of the fixation of dehydration again aquation.Again preferably about 5 DEG C to about 35 DEG C of the temperature of aquation.The pearl of generated aquation again can be directly used for the reaction that glycolic is produced from glycollic nitrile, or be stored in hydrated liquid again at about 5 DEG C to about 35 DEG C until using.  
 
 Glycollic nitrile is hydrolyzed to glycolic using nitrilase catalyst 
 
 Glycollic nitrile can be performed such that under suitable reaction condition as described below (i.e. in the aqueous reaction mixture of certain pH range, temperature, concentration etc.) to the enzymatic conversion method of glycolic (form of acid and/or corresponding ammonium salt) and contact with the enzyme catalyst of the enzyme catalyst of enzyme catalyst, fixation with nitrilase activity or the fixation of crosslinking.In one embodiment, by entire recombinant microorganism cell with glutaraldehyde pretreatment, fixed, crosslinking, dehydration in carrageenan, again the enzyme catalyst generated after aquation is directly used in conversion of the glycollic nitrile to glycolic, alternatively, doughnut film roll or ultrafiltration membrane, which can be used, individually retains revocable cell from large (bulk) reaction mixture.In the second embodiment, entire recombinant microorganism cell is fixed in polyacrylamide gel, generated enzyme catalyst is directly used in conversion of the glycollic nitrile to glycolic.  
 The concentration of enzyme catalyst in aqueous reaction mixture depends on the specific activity of enzyme catalyst and is selected according to the reaction rate gone for.It is used as the wet cell weight of the microbial cell of catalyst in hydrolysis generally between the wet cell for having 0.001 gram to 0.250 gram in every milliliter of total reaction volume, preferably every milliliter 0.002 gram to 0.050 gram of wet cell.Wet cell weight percentage in the total reaction volume of the every volume indicated can be present in reaction mixture in the form of fixed enzyme catalyst (prepare (see above) as described above), wherein can learn the weight of the wet cell as fixed enzyme catalyst total weight percentage from the method for the fixed enzyme catalyst of preparation.  
 The temperature of ethyl alcohol nitrile hydrolysis reactor is chosen to be and not only controls reaction rate but also controls the active stability of enzyme catalyst.The temperature of reaction may is that the freezing point (about 0 DEG C) of slightly higher than reaction mixture to about 65 DEG C, and preferred range of reaction temperature is about 5 DEG C to about 35 DEG C.It can (the initial pH of reaction will be maintained at about 5.0 to about 10.0 by it by the way that the cell of the fixation of dehydration to be suspended in the aqueous solution of distilled water or buffer, preferably approximately 5.5 to about 8.0, more preferably from about 5.5 to about 7.7, most preferably from about 6.0 to preparing enzyme catalyst suspension in about 7.7).With the progress of reaction, the pH of reaction mixture will change, this is because foring the ammonium salt of carboxylic acid from corresponding nitrile functionality.Reaction can be proceeded to the conversion for fully achieving glycollic nitrile without controlling pH, or suitable acid or alkali can be added with the process of reaction to keep desired pH.  
 It was found that glycollic nitrile is at 25 DEG C with arbitrary proportion and water complete miscibility.Concentration (buffer or the product ethanol acid ammonium salt of salt in the temperature and/or water phase that the dissolubility that reaction condition is chosen to be substrate (i.e. alpha-hydroxy nitrile) also relies on solution, also referred to as alcohol acid phosphate) in the case where, initial reaction mixture can be by two phase compositions: the water phase and organic phase (undissolved alpha-hydroxy nitrile) of the alpha-hydroxy nitrile containing enzyme catalyst and dissolution.With the progress of reaction, alpha-hydroxy nitrile is dissolved into water phase, the final product mixtures for obtaining single-phase.Reaction can also be performed such that be approximately equal to the rate of enzymatic hydrolysis reaction rate and alpha-hydroxy nitrile is added into reaction mixture, to keep the aqueous reaction mixture of single-phase, and avoid the potential problems of the substrate suppression of enzyme in the starting material of high concentration.  
 Glycolic can be used as protonated carboxylic acid and/or its corresponding ammonium salt (pH depending on product mixtures；The pKa of glycolic is that mixture about 3.83) is present in product mixtures, in addition can be used as the salt of carboxylic acid and any buffer that may be additionally present of in product mixtures and exists.In general, the glycolic generated is mainly the form of ammonium salt (pH of ethyl alcohol nitrile hydrolysis reactor is typically about 5.5 to about 7.7).As needed, glycolic acid product can be separated from reaction mixture in the form of protonated carboxylic acid or carboxylate.  
 When glycollic nitrile converts completely in product mixtures glycolic final concentration of 0.001M to glycolic acid product upper solubility limit.In one embodiment, the concentration of glycolic is about 0.10M to about 5.0M.In another embodiment, the concentration of glycolic is about 0.2M to about 3.0M.  
 Multiple technologies (including but not limited to, ion exchange, electrodialysis, reactive solvents extraction, polymerization, thermal decomposition, alcoholysis, and combinations thereof) can be used and recycle glycolic in the form of acid or corresponding salt.

 Correspond to analytical unit in specification, technology, the abbreviation of property or compound is as follows: " sec " means the second, " min " means minute, " h " or " hr " means hour, " d " means the density indicated with g/mL, " μ L " is meant microlitre, " mL " means milliliter, " L " means liter, " mM " is meant mM, " M " is meant mole, " mmol " means mmoles, " wt " means weight, " wt% " means weight percent, " g " is meant gram, " μ g " means microgram, " HPLC " means high performance liquid chromatography, " O.D. " means the optical density in specified wavelength, " dcw " means stem cell weight, " U " means nitrilase activity units, " EDTA " means second two Amine tetraacethyl, " DTT " mean dithiothreitol (DTT).The nitrilase activity of one unit corresponds to the glycollic nitrile of 1 μm of ol of hydrolysis per minute.  
 
 Analysis method 
 
 HPLC analysis 
 Unless otherwise specified, HPLC method below is otherwise used.Pass through the product mixtures of following HPLC method analysis reaction.The equal portions (0.01mL) of reaction mixture are added into 1.50mL water and (HPX 87H column, 30cmx7.8mm are analyzed by HPLC；0.01N H 2 SO 4 Mobile phase；50 DEG C, flow velocity 1.0mL/min；10 μ L volume injecteds；RI detector, 20 minute analysis time).Using the commercially glycollic nitrile bought from Aldrich be serially diluted calibration method carried out for glycollic nitrile.  
 It is quantitative 13 CNMR analysis 
 It is quantified using Varian Unity Inova spectrometer (Varian, Inc., Palo Alto, CA) in 400MHz 13 CNMR spectrum.Sample preparation: 3.0mL reaction product and 0.5mL D are added in the NMR pipe of 10mm 2 O.It is obtained usually using the spectrum width (transmitter is located at 100ppm, 128K point) and 90 degree of pulses (pw90=10.7 microsecond when emitted energy is 56db) of 26KHz 13 CNMR spectrum.Longest 13C T1 (23sec) and GLN nitrile carbon phase are closed, and total cycle time is set as (circulation delay d1=240sec, acquisition time at=2.52sec) 10 times bigger than the numerical value.Signal averaging is total experimental period that 26.3 hours are provided when 360 scanning.Gating only is decoupled to the 1H that Waltz- is adjusted during acquisition time (at), to inhibit Nuclear Overhauser Enhancement (NOE).  
 
 The fermentation of 1 Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V of embodiment 
 
 Before being inoculated into fermentor, 6-10h (OD is grown in (300rpm) 500mL LB culture medium (every milliliter of supplement 0.1mg ampicillin) that the inoculum of Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V shakes at 30 DEG C 550 =1-2).Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V nitrilase strain growth is in 14-L Braun Biostat C fermentor (B.Braun Biotech InternationalGmbh, Melsungen, Germany in), the most simple culture medium of use (wherein containing glucose, ammonia and salt and for the lactose of induction).Sterilizing primary fermentation culture medium (7.5L) is described in table 2.Additive after sterilizing includes trace element (table 3), every milliliter of 0.1mg ampicillin, every liter of 2g casamino acid (Difco), every liter of 4g glucose and the 500mL inoculum of filtration sterilization.  
 Table 4 describes fermentation set point.NH 4 OH (40%w/v) and H 3 PO 4 (20%w/v) is for controlling pH.By Dissolved Oxygen concentration Control the 25% of the saturation of the air, as the increase of oxygen demand improves stirring setting first, then ventilate.It has been given in Table 5 lactose induction feeding medium during fermentation program used.If glucose is accumulated over 5g/L, glucose feed rate is reduced.After 40-56 hours, fermentation liquid is cooled to 5-10 DEG C, by the way that cell is collected by centrifugation.Cell is pasted and freezes and is stored in -70 DEG C.Cell paste is named as NIT 60 (1910 GLN U/g dcw).

 Fixation of the 2 Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V of embodiment in the carrageenan pearl that GA/PEI is crosslinked 
 
 At 50 DEG C, 12g carrageenan (FMC GP911) is slowly added into 228g deionized-distilled water when stirring rapidly, by obtained mixture be heated to 80 DEG C until carrageenan be completely dissolved, by obtained solution stirring be cooled to 52 DEG C.In the beaker individually with stirrer, at about 25 DEG C, to 84.8g 0.35M Na 2 HPO 4 The Escherichia coli MG1655/pNM18-168V cell (25.2%dcw) of 83.2g freezing is added in (pH 7.3) and mixes until cell suspends, then deoxyribonuclease I solution (10 μ L 12,500U/mL DNase (Sigma)/100mL cell suspending liquid) is added.Cell suspending liquid is continued through into 230 microns and 140 microns of Nupro TF strainer elementfilter filterings, and is heated with stirring to 50 DEG C.While agitating, 50 DEG C of 160.0g Escherichia coli MG1655/pNM18-168V cell suspending liquid is added in 52 DEG C of Carrageenan solution, obtained cell/carrageenan suspension is pumped into the syringe needle of electrically heated 20G at 47 DEG C, instills 0.25M KHCO while agitating at about 37-38 DEG C 3 (pH=7.3)；Flow rate set by syringe needle is 5-8mL/min.The pearl made hardens 1 hour in identical buffer in room temperature while agitating, is stored at 0.25M saleratus (pH 7.3).  
 The chemical crosslinking of fixed cell/carrageenan pearl, which is performed such that, is added to the glutaraldehyde (GA) (Sigma M752-07) of the 0.5 g  25% in water in the 20g pearl being suspended in 48mL 0.25M saleratus (pH 7.3), and 1 hour is stirred at room temperature.Then the polyethyleneimine (PEI, BASF LUPASOL PS) for the 2.0g 12.5wt% being added to the water into bead suspension, is stirred for 18 hours for bead suspension in room temperature.The pearl that GA/PEI crosslinking is recycled from suspension, is stirred twice (15 minutes) in 48mL 0.25M saleratus (pH 7.3)；It is then stored in 5 DEG C of 1.0M ammonium hydrogen carbonate (pH 7.3).Before being used as glycollic nitrile and being converted into the catalyst of glycolic (as ammonium salt), pearl is washed twice to remove 1.0M ammonium hydrogen carbonate (pH 7.3) store buffer liquid by (15 minutes) with 180mL 0.1M alcohol acid phosphate (pH 7.3) in room temperature.The cell catalyst of obtained fixation is referred to as fixed NIT 60.  
 
 The aquation of the dehydration of the fixed Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-F168V transformant of the carrageenan of 3 glutaraldehydes of embodiment/polyethyleneimine crosslinking/again 
 
 The 35 DEG C of dehydration of Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138- F168V transformant pearl  24 hours for fixing the glutaraldehyde prepared as described in Example 2/polyethyleneimine crosslinking carrageenan in the vacuum tank (176mm Hg) purged with nitrogen.The ratio of pearl weight and initial (not being dehydrated) pearl weight is 0.0914 after dehydration.Then in (by weight) the 0.10M alcohol acid phosphate solution (pH 7.3) for dewatered pearl being placed in 20 times at 5 DEG C or 25 DEG C, thus by the pearl of dehydration again aquation.The pearl of obtained aquation again is washed twice with 9 times of (by weight) 0.10M alcohol acid phosphate solution (pH 7.3), is then weighed；It is carried out for the pearl of aquation again at 5 DEG C, the ratio of the pearl weight of aquation and initial (not being dehydrated) pearl weight is 0.210 again；It is carried out for the pearl of aquation again at 25 DEG C, the ratio of the pearl weight of aquation and initial pearl weight is 0.212 again.

 Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V is pre-processed with glutaraldehyde before  embodiment  5 is fixed 
 
 The fermentation of 200-L is carried out to generate the fermentation liquid containing Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V cell, then before fixing in situ with glutaraldehyde pretreatment cell.Pre- inoculum is prepared first: 0.5L seed culture medium being added in the shaking flask of 2-L (containing yeast extract (Ambrex 695,5.0g/L), K 2 HPO 4 (10.0g/L), KH 2 PO 4 (7.0g/L), trisodium citrate dihydrate (1.0g/L), (NH 4 ) 2 SO 4 (4.0g/L), MgSO 4 ·7H 2 O (1.0g/L) and ferric citrate (0.10g/L)).The pH of culture medium is adjusted to 6.8, culture medium is sterilized in bottle.Additive includes glucose (10mL, 50wt%) and 1mL ampicillin (25mg/mL) after sterilizing.The Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V stock culture of 1-mL freezing in 20% glycerol is inoculated into pre- seed culture medium, and is cultivated at 35 DEG C and 300rpm.In about 2OD 550 The seed fermenter (Braun) that inoculum is transferred to 14L (wherein containing the culture medium of 8L, is contained into KH in culture medium 2 PO 4 (3.50g/L), FeSO 4 ·7H 2 O (0.05g/L), MgSO 4 ·7H 2 O (2.0g/L), trisodium citrate dihydrate (1.90g/L), yeast extract (Ambrex 695,5.0g/L), Biospumex153K defrother (0.25mL/L, CognisCorporation), NaCl (1.0g/L), CaCl 2 ·2H 2 O (10g/L) and NIT trace element solution (10mL/L)).Trace element solution contains monohydrate potassium (10g/L), is hydrated MnSO 4 (2g/L), NaCl (2g/L), FeSO 4 ·7H 2 O (0.5g/L), ZnSO 4 ·7H 2 O (0.2g/L), CuSO 4 ·5H 2 O (0.02g/L) and NaMoO 4 ·2H 2 O(0.02g/L).Additive includes 120g glucose solution (50%w/w) and ampicillin 16mL storage liquid (25mg/mL) after sterilizing.  
 The concentration of dissolved oxygen (dO) is controlled the 25% of the saturation of the air.DO then is controlled by Ventilation Rate (2 to 10slpm) by impeller stirring rate (400 to 1400rpm) first.PH is controlled 6.8.NH 4 OH (29%w/w) and H 2 SO 4 (20%w/v) is for controlling pH.By temperature control at 35 DEG C, head pressure is 0.5bars.In ca 6OD 550 When culture is transferred to the Biostat-D Braun fermentor of 200L.Culture medium used is identical as in seed fermenter, and initialization volume is 140L, and 50%w/w glucose is added to 8g/L.Starting fermentation is operated with batch first, once glucose consumption then starts fed-batch operation according to predetermined rate (table 6) with 50%w/w glucose to < 0.5g/L.In ca 25OD 550 When, feed supplement is converted into the 25%D- lactose solution (table 7) according to predetermined rate.  
 By temperature control at 35.0 DEG C, the control of head pressure is in 0.5bar, and 6.8, the pH of second stage (lactose stage) is controlled 7.2 for the pH control of first stage (glucose stage).NH 4 OH (29%w/w) and H 2 SO 4 (20%w/v) for controlling pH, the 25% of the saturation of the air, the dO of second stage is controlled 10% for the dO control of first stage.First then dO is controlled by ventilation (25 to 35slpm) by stirring (250 to 450rpm).Glucose and lactose level are monitored during feed operation, it is interim to stop feed regimes or reduce feed supplement if glucose level is more than 0.1g/L or lactose is more than 1g/L.Operation terminates after starting lactose feed supplement 40 hours, collects cell by centrifugation or microfiltration or keeps carrying out glutaraldehyde processing in a reservoir.The fermentation of generation is about 8kg stem cell weight, the nitrilase specific activity with 2819BZN U/g dcw (1788 GLN U/g dcw).

 The final cell suspension liquid concentrate recycled in the fermentation liquid of the  embodiment  5 handled from glutaraldehyde and sodium hydrogensulfite is centrifuged at 5 DEG C.The cell precipitation of generation is resuspended in the 0.35M kaliumphosphate buffer (pH 7.2) of 5 times of weight, obtained cell suspending liquid is centrifuged at 5 DEG C, is pasted to generate fixed and GA and PEI chemical crosslinking wet cell as described in Example 2.The cell catalyst of the fixation of generation is referred to as fixed NIT 188A-C2.

 In Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138- F168V transformant pearl  20 hours of dehydration that 35 DEG C are fixed the glutaraldehyde prepared as described in example 6 above/polyethyleneimine crosslinking carrageenan in the vacuum tank (176mm Hg) purged with nitrogen, weighing, is dehydrated 4 hours (in total 24 hours) again in a manner described.The ratio of pearl weight and initial (not being dehydrated) pearl weight is 0.217 after dehydration.Then pearl is placed in 72 hours in 20 times of (by weight) 0.10M alcohol acid phosphate solution (pH 7.3) at 5 DEG C, thus by the pearl of dehydration again aquation.The pearl of obtained aquation again is washed twice with 9 times of (by weight) 0.10M alcohol acid phosphate solution (pH 7.3), is then weighed；It is carried out for the pearl of aquation again at 5 DEG C, the ratio of the pearl weight of aquation and initial (not being dehydrated) pearl weight is 0.578 again.The biocatalyst of generation is referred to as fixed NIT 188A-C2-D.  
 
 Specific activity of the  embodiment  8 using the fixed Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-F168V biocatalyst of glutaraldehyde/polyethyleneimine crosslinking carrageenan of the pretreated Escherichia coli MG1655/pNM18-168V Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-F168V transformant preparation of glutaraldehyde before and after fixed biocatalyst dehydration/aquation again 
 
 In typical program, glycollic nitrile is carried out in the jacketed reactor (there is top agitating device, temperature is controlled at 25 DEG C) of 50mL and reacts (every group duplicate) to glycolate converting batch.In first group of double reaction, Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V/ carrageenan pearl (the 0.20g stem cell weight of 4g GA/PEI crosslinking is added in each reactor；Fixed NIT188A-C2, prepares (use GA pretreatment cell before fixed) as described in Example 6), the deionized-distilled water of aqueous ethanol acid ammonium (4.0M, the pH 7.0) and 7.75mL of 3.0mL.In second group of double reaction, Escherichia coli MG1655/pSW138-168V/ carrageenan pearl (the 0.20g stem cell weight of 2.55g GA/PEI crosslinking is added in each reactor；Fixed NIT188A-C2-D, as described in Example 7 preparation (GA pretreatment cell being used before fixed, then the aquation of dehydration/again)), the deionized-distilled water of aqueous ethanol acid ammonium (4.0M, the pH 7.0) and 9.10mL of 3.0mL.  
 Each reactor is rinsed with nitrogen, in 25 DEG C of stirring mixtures, while 0.520mL 62wt% glycollic nitrile (GLN) (6.0mmol GLN, the 0.006mmol formaldehyde for pumping while being added to the water using programmed injector；With 0.7wt% glycolic stablize) and 0.150mL watery ammonium hydroxide (0.9375wt%NH 3 )；1 part of isometric GLN and Ammonia (8 GLN solution and watery ammonium hydroxide is added simultaneously in total) is added to keep the concentration≤400mM and pH of GLN in the range of 7.0-7.5 in every 2 hours simultaneously.After being initially added GLN in the 0.25M isopropanol (HPLC external perimysium reference) of predetermined time taking-up response sample (0.050mL) and the 6.0N HCl and the 0.200mL in water that add to 0.010mL, obtained mixture is centrifuged, supernatant is analyzed to determine the specific activity (μm ol glycolic/min/g dcw biocatalyst) of initial reaction rate and catalyst by HPLC.When reacting completion, 100% GLN is converted to generate glycolic (in the form of ammonium salt), yield > 99%.Table 9 lists the initial specific activity of biocatalyst.  
 At the end that first is reacted, aqueous product mixture (under a nitrogen) is fallen off from the catalyst in each reactor, leaves the mixture of fixed cell catalyst and residual product solution.Then enough deionized-distilled waters are added into reactor, to make the initial reaction volume in first reaction restore (the initial reaction volume of about 15.3mL) before GLN and Ammonia is added, the equal portions (as described in the preceding paragraph immediately) by the way that aqueous GLN and ammonium hydroxide is added carry out second reaction at 25 DEG C.The specific activity of the biocatalyst recycled in the continuous batch reaction with catalyst circulation is listed in table 10.

 Storage stability of the  embodiment  9 using the fixed biocatalyst of glutaraldehyde/polyethyleneimine crosslinking carrageenan of the pretreated Escherichia coli MG1655/pNM18-168V transformant preparation of glutaraldehyde before and after fixed biocatalyst dehydration/aquation again
